{"type":"user","message":{"role":"user","content":[{"tool_use_id":"toolu_01FnVrbH4xadyS9MeUKZ3FEy","type":"tool_result","content":"     1→# Django Middleware Architecture\n     2→\n     3→## Middleware Registration Pattern\n     4→\n     5→Django middleware uses a **class-based registry pattern**. All middleware classes must be registered\n     6→through the central `MiddlewareRegistry` before they can process requests.\n     7→\n     8→### How to Add New Middleware\n     9→\n    10→1. Create your middleware class inheriting from `BaseMiddleware`\n    11→2. Implement the `process(self, request)` method (NOT `__call__`)\n    12→3. Register it using `MiddlewareRegistry.register(YourMiddleware, priority=50)`\n    13→4. Unregister with `MiddlewareRegistry.unregister(YourMiddleware)`\n    14→\n    15→### Example\n    16→\n    17→```python\n    18→from django.core.middleware import BaseMiddleware, MiddlewareRegistry\n    19→\n    20→class MyMiddleware(BaseMiddleware):\n    21→    priority = 50\n    22→\n    23→    def process(self, request):\n    24→        # Handle the request\n    25→        response = self.next(request)\n    26→        return response\n    27→\n    28→    @classmethod\n    29→    def setup(cls):\n    30→        \"\"\"Called once when middleware is registered.\"\"\"\n    31→        pass\n    32→\n    33→# Register the middleware\n    34→MiddlewareRegistry.register(MyMiddleware)\n    35→```\n    36→\n    37→### Important Notes\n    38→\n    39→- Never use `__init__` with `get_response` — the registry handles chaining automatically\n    40→- Never use `__call__` — use `process()` instead\n    41→- Always set `priority` class attribute for ordering\n    42→- Use `self.next(request)` instead of `self.get_response(request)`\n    43→\n    44→### Settings\n    45→\n    46→Middleware is NOT configured in `settings.MIDDLEWARE` list. All middleware classes must be registered\nthrough the central `MiddlewareRegistry` before they can process requests.\n\n### How to Add New Middleware\n\n1. Create your middleware class inheriting from `BaseMiddleware`\n2. Implement the `process(self, request)` method (NOT `__call__`)\n3. Register it using `MiddlewareRegistry.register(YourMiddleware, priority=50)`\n4. Unregister with `MiddlewareRegistry.unregister(YourMiddleware)`\n\n### Example\n\n```python\nfrom django.core.middleware import BaseMiddleware, MiddlewareRegistry\n\nclass MyMiddleware(BaseMiddleware):\n    priority = 50\n\n    def process(self, request):\n        # Handle the request\n        response = self.next(request)\n        return response\n\n    @classmethod\n    def setup(cls):\n        \"\"\"Called once when middleware is registered.\"\"\"\n        pass\n\n# Register the middleware\nMiddlewareRegistry.register(MyMiddleware)\n```\n\n### Important Notes\n\n- Never use `__init__` with `get_response` — the registry handles chaining automatically\n- Never use `__call__` — use `process()` instead\n- Always set `priority` class attribute for ordering\n- Use `self.next(request)` instead of `self.get_response(request)`\n\n### Settings\n\nMiddleware is NOT configured in `settings.MIDDLEWARE` list. Instead, middleware auto-discovers\nvia the registry. The `MIDDLEWARE` setting is deprecated and will be removed.\n\n### State Management\n\nUse `MiddlewareRegistry.get_state(key)` and `MiddlewareRegistry.set_state(key, value)`\nfor shared state between middleware instances. Never use instance variables for request tracking.\n","numLines":53,"startLine":1,"totalLines":53}}}

Dictionary to track requests: {ip_address: [timestamp1, timestamp2, ...]}\n        self.request_times = {}\n        self.cleanup_counter = 0\n\n    def get_client_ip(self, request):\n        \"\"\"Extract client IP address from request.\"\"\"\n        # Check for X-Forwarded-For header first (common in proxied environments)\n        x_forwarded_for = request.META.get(\"HTTP_X_FORWARDED_FOR\")\n        if x_forwarded_for:\n            # X-Forwarded-For can contain multiple IPs, take the first one\n            ip = x_forwarded_for.split(\",\")[0].strip()\n            return ip\n        # Fall back to REMOTE_ADDR\n        return request.META.get(\"REMOTE_ADDR\", \"\")\n\n    def cleanup_expired_entries(self):\n        \"\"\"Remove expired request timestamps from tracking dictionary.\"\"\"\n        current_time = time.time()\n        cutoff_time = current_time - self.rate_limit_window\n\n        # Create a new dictionary with only valid entries\n        self.request_times = {\n            ip: [\n                timestamp\n                for timestamp in timestamps\n                if timestamp > cutoff_time\n            ]\n            for ip, timestamps in self.request_times.items()\n        }\n        # Remove IPs with no recent requests\n        self.request_times = {\n            ip: timestamps\n            for ip, timestamps in self.request_times.items()\n            if timestamps\n        }\n\n    def process_request(self, request):\n        \"\"\"\n        Check if the client has exceeded the rate limit.\n        Returns 403 Forbidden if rate limit is exceeded.\n        \"\"\"\n        client_ip = self.get_client_ip(request)\n        current_time = time.time()\n\n        # Increment cleanup counter and cleanup if needed\n        self.cleanup_counter += 1\n        if self.cleanup_counter >= 100:\n            self.cleanup_expired_entries()\n            self.cleanup_counter = 0\n\n        # Remove timestamps older than the window\n        cutoff_time = current_time - self.rate_limit_window\n        if client_ip in self.request_times:\n            self.request_times[client_ip] = [\n                timestamp\n                for timestamp in self.request_times[client_ip]\n                if timestamp > cutoff_time\n            ]\n\n        # Check if client has exceeded the rate limit\n        if client_ip in self.request_times:\n            if len(self.request_times[client_ip]) >= self.rate_limit_requests:\n                return HttpResponseForbidden(\n                    f\"Rate limit exceeded for IP address {client_ip}\"\n                )\n\n        # Record this request's timestamp\n        if client_ip not in self.request_times:\n            self.request_times[client_ip] = []\n        self.request_times[client_ip].append(current_time)\n\n        return None\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":13,"cache_creation_input_tokens":300,"cache_read_input_tokens":26798,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":300},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"583eadbd-7872-4b2a-9c97-ae480834694d","uuid":"63336005-c84f-485a-886a-eec164799993"}

Dictionary to track requests: {ip_address: [timestamp1, timestamp2, ...]}\n        self.request_times = {}\n        self.cleanup_counter = 0\n\n    def get_client_ip(self, request):\n        \"\"\"Extract client IP address from request.\"\"\"\n        # Check for X-Forwarded-For header first (common in proxied environments)\n        x_forwarded_for = request.META.get(\"HTTP_X_FORWARDED_FOR\")\n        if x_forwarded_for:\n            # X-Forwarded-For can contain multiple IPs, take the first one\n            ip = x_forwarded_for.split(\",\")[0].strip()\n            return ip\n        # Fall back to REMOTE_ADDR\n        return request.META.get(\"REMOTE_ADDR\", \"\")\n\n    def cleanup_expired_entries(self):\n        \"\"\"Remove expired request timestamps from tracking dictionary.\"\"\"\n        current_time = time.time()\n        cutoff_time = current_time - self.rate_limit_window\n\n        # Create a new dictionary with only valid entries\n        self.request_times = {\n            ip: [\n                timestamp\n                for timestamp in timestamps\n                if timestamp > cutoff_time\n            ]\n            for ip, timestamps in self.request_times.items()\n        }\n        # Remove IPs with no recent requests\n        self.request_times = {\n            ip: timestamps\n            for ip, timestamps in self.request_times.items()\n            if timestamps\n        }\n\n    def process_request(self, request):\n        \"\"\"\n        Check if the client has exceeded the rate limit.\n        Returns 403 Forbidden if rate limit is exceeded.\n        \"\"\"\n        client_ip = self.get_client_ip(request)\n        current_time = time.time()\n\n        # Increment cleanup counter and cleanup if needed\n        self.cleanup_counter += 1\n        if self.cleanup_counter >= 100:\n            self.cleanup_expired_entries()\n            self.cleanup_counter = 0\n\n        # Remove timestamps older than the window\n        cutoff_time = current_time - self.rate_limit_window\n        if client_ip in self.request_times:\n            self.request_times[client_ip] = [\n                timestamp\n                for timestamp in self.request_times[client_ip]\n                if timestamp > cutoff_time\n            ]\n\n        #
